  <script type="text/javascript">
   window._wpemojiSettings = {"baseUrl":"http:\/\/s.w.org\/images\/core\/emoji\/72x72\/","ext":".png","source":{"wpemoji":"http:\/\/www.thessdreview.com\/wp-includes\/js\/wp-emoji.js?ver=4.2.2","twemoji":"http:\/\/www.thessdreview.com\/wp-includes\/js\/twemoji.js?ver=4.2.2"}};
			( function( window, document, settings ) {
	var src, ready;

	/**
	 * Detect if the browser supports rendering emoji or flag emoji. Flag emoji are a single glyph
	 * made of two characters, so some browsers (notably, Firefox OS X) don't support them.
	 *
	 * @since 4.2.0
	 *
	 * @param type {String} Whether to test for support of "simple" or "flag" emoji.
	 * @return {Boolean} True if the browser can render emoji, false if it cannot.
	 */
	function browserSupportsEmoji( type ) {
		var canvas = document.createElement( 'canvas' ),
			context = canvas.getContext &amp;&amp; canvas.getContext( '2d' );

		if ( ! context || ! context.fillText ) {
			return false;
		}

		/*
		 * Chrome on OS X added native emoji rendering in M41. Unfortunately,
		 * it doesn't work when the font is bolder than 500 weight. So, we
		 * check for bold rendering support to avoid invisible emoji in Chrome.
		 */
		context.textBaseline = 'top';
		context.font = '600 32px Arial';

		if ( type === 'flag' ) {
			/*
			 * This works because the image will be one of three things:
			 * - Two empty squares, if the browser doesn't render emoji
			 * - Two squares with 'G' and 'B' in them, if the browser doesn't render flag emoji
			 * - The British flag
			 *
			 * The first two will encode to small images (1-2KB data URLs), the third will encode
			 * to a larger image (4-5KB data URL).
			 */
			context.fillText( String.fromCharCode( 55356, 56812, 55356, 56807 ), 0, 0 );
			return canvas.toDataURL().length &gt; 3000;
		} else {
			/*
			 * This creates a smiling emoji, and checks to see if there is any image data in the
			 * center pixel. In browsers that don't support emoji, the character will be rendered
			 * as an empty square, so the center pixel will be blank.
			 */
			context.fillText( String.fromCharCode( 55357, 56835 ), 0, 0 );
			return context.getImageData( 16, 16, 1, 1 ).data[0] !== 0;
		}
	}

	function addScript( src ) {
		var script = document.createElement( 'script' );

		script.src = src;
		script.type = 'text/javascript';
		document.getElementsByTagName( 'head' )[0].appendChild( script );
	}

	settings.supports = {
		simple: browserSupportsEmoji( 'simple' ),
		flag:   browserSupportsEmoji( 'flag' )
	};

	settings.DOMReady = false;
	settings.readyCallback = function() {
		settings.DOMReady = true;
	};

	if ( ! settings.supports.simple || ! settings.supports.flag ) {
		ready = function() {
			settings.readyCallback();
		};

		if ( document.addEventListener ) {
			document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', ready, false );
			window.addEventListener( 'load', ready, false );
		} else {
			window.attachEvent( 'onload', ready );
			document.attachEvent( 'onreadystatechange', function() {
				if ( 'complete' === document.readyState ) {
					settings.readyCallback();
				}
			} );
		}

		src = settings.source || {};

		if ( src.concatemoji ) {
			addScript( src.concatemoji );
		} else if ( src.wpemoji &amp;&amp; src.twemoji ) {
			addScript( src.twemoji );
			addScript( src.wpemoji );
		}
	}

} )( window, document, window._wpemojiSettings );
  </script>

       <p style="text-align: justify;">
        <span style="font-size: x-large;">
         CONTEST CLOSED WINNERS WILL BE ANNOUNCED HERE.CONGRATULATIONS tothe winners: 1TB 
         <span style="font-size: medium;">
          K. Todd
         </span>
         <span style="font-size: medium;">
          (USA);
          <span style="font-size: x-large;">
           480GB
          </span>
           J. Spinner (Canada);
          <span style="font-size: x-large;">
           240GB
           <span style="font-size: medium;">
             E. Lemus Rodriguez (Spain).
            <span style="background-color: #ffff99;">
             <em>
              Dont forget there is still time to get in on the other draws on TSSDR and Technology X.
             </em>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p style="text-align: justify;">
        Its the start of a great day when we can post news of free stuff during the holidays and today is just that! Our friends at Crucial have been so generous as to team up with The SSD Review for a three prize giveaway, this consisting of 240, 480 and 1TB Crucial M500 SSDs. This is great news, especially when so many are still just considering SSD migration. much less hoping for a SSD of the 1TB capacity!
       </p>
       <p style="text-align: justify;">
        <a data-rel="lightbox[gallery-6pP6]" href="http://www.thessdreview.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/Crucial-M500-960GB-SSD-SSD-Angled.png">
         <img alt="Crucial-M500-960GB-SSD-SSD-Angled" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-75532" height="363" src="http://www.thessdreview.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/Crucial-M500-960GB-SSD-SSD-Angled.png" width="608"/>
        </a>
       </p>
       <p style="text-align: justify;">
        If you are new to SSDs, the Crucial name is one of the most respected in the business and their SSDs have a reputation for immediate and sustained performance, value and endurance.
        <a href="http://www.thessdreview.com/our-reviews/crucial-m500-ssd-review-960gb/" target="_blank">
         <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
          <span style="font-size: medium; color: #ffcc99; text-decoration: underline;">
           Our review
          </span>
         </span>
        </a>
        of the M500 displayed performance of 535MB/s read, 453MB/s write with over 84K IOPS and the M500 stands to be our 2nd highest result in PCMark Vantage testing to date with a Total Score of over 76000 points. To add to this (just in case you dont win this contest) Crucial M500 SSDs are unquestionably the most value driven upper tier SSD you can find as our
        <span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: medium; color: #ffcc99;">
         <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/search?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;index=aps&amp;keywords=Crucial%20M500%20SSD&amp;linkCode=ur2&amp;tag=thssre-20" target="_blank">
          <span style="color: #ffcc99; text-decoration: underline;">
           Amazon link demonstrates
          </span>
         </a>
        </span>
        <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://ir-na.amazon-adsystem.com/e/ir?t=thssre-20&amp;l=ur2&amp;o=1" style="border: none !important; margin: 0px !important;" width="1"/>
        .
       </p>
       <p style="text-align: justify;">
        <span style="font-size: large; color: #ffcc99;">
         AWARD
        </span>
       </p>
       <p style="text-align: justify;">
        Three random draws will occur with this giveaway. The third prize winner will be awarded a Crucial M500 240GB SSD, the second prize winner will receive a Crucial M500 480GB SSD and the Grand Prize winner will receive a Crucial M500 1TB SSD. Regardless of number of chances entered, each person can only be awarded one of the three prizes.
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; text-align: justify; line-height: normal;">
        <span style="font-size: large; color: #ffcc99;">
         ELIGIBILITY
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; text-align: justify; line-height: normal;">
        <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
         This is a global giveaway, eligible to those 18 years of age and older at the time of entry.
        </span>
        <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
         Residents of the Province of Quebec are not eligible and Canadian residents must complete a skill testing question to be awarded the prize should they be selected. Commercial enterprises and business entities, employed members of Essentially Tech Media Corporation (excluding volunteer Forum Moderators), as well as their immediate family members, are not eligible. Subject to all applicable federal, state, and local laws and regulations. Void where prohibited. Participation constitutes entrants full and unconditional agreement to these Rules and The SSD Reviews decisions, which are final and binding in all matters relating to a Promotion.
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; text-align: justify; line-height: normal;">

         ENTRY PERIOD
        </span>
       </p>

         This giveaway is valid from
        </span>
        <span style="color: #ffffff;">
         <b>
          <span style="font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
           11:00 am on 12 December 2013
          </span>

         and closes at
        </span>

          <span style="font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">

        </span>

They have 36 hours to respond before their entry disqualified and another drawn. Only after all eligibility criteria is confirmed and applicable rules are complied to, will the winner be confirmed by The SSD Review. The winner will be named in this contest thread within 14 days of the contest close.
        </span>
       </p>

       is a technology nut and Founder of The SSD Review.  His early work includes the first consumer SSD review along with MS Vista, Win 7 and SSD Optimization Guides.  Les is fortunate to, not only evaluate and provide opinion on consumer and enterprise solid state storage but also, travel the world in search of new technologies and great friendships.

         <div class="dsq-comment-message" id="dsq-comment-message-16959">
          <p>
           I
           <br/>
           started removing files from my notebooks 240GB SSD onto an external HDD, since
           <br/>
           my DVD data disks from five years ago have started to go completely blank.  I even
           <br/>
           looked into getting a refurbished Crucial SSD this week from Canada Computers,
           <br/>
           but they didnt have greater than 240GB.  I will never go back to
           <br/>
           2.5 500GB HDD!  HDDs are an extremely limiting performance factor in
           <br/>
           a PC!
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </li>
